<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́ветрить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vývetritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to disappear, to be forgotten <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of thoughts, feelings, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>

***вывод.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вывод.html>вы́вод</a> (1503)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вывод.html>вы́вод</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vývod</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вывод.html>вы́вода</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вывод.html>вы́воды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вывод.html>вы́водов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>withdrawal</li>
<li>conclusion, inference, deduction</li>
<li>derivation</li>
<li>outlet, leading-out wire</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выводившийся.html>выводи́вшийся</a> (27433)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***выводить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выводить.html>вы́водить</a> (4313)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:водить.html>води́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выводить.html>выводи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vyvodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вывести.html>вы́вести</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to take out, to lead out, to bring out, to move out; to help out <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">help somebody to get off</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выводить.html>выводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чистый.html>чи́стую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>во́ду</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vyvodítʹ</b> na čístuju vódu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bring out into the open, to expose, to unmask, to show up</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to withdraw, to call off (troops)</li>
<li>to derive, to conclude, to infer, to deduce
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выводить.html>выводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:формула.html>фо́рмулу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vyvodítʹ</b> fórmulu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to deduce / derive a formula</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to remove
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выводить.html>выводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:состав.html>соста́ва</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:президиум.html>прези́диума</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vyvodítʹ</b> iz sostáva prezídiuma</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to <b>remove</b> from the presidium</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выводить.html>выводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vyvodítʹ</b> iz sebjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to drive smb. out of his wits, to drive smb. to distraction; to drive smb. crazy</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">to <b>remove</b> (someone) from himself/herself</span>”)</div>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́та</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробка.html>про́бка</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:выводить.html>выво́дит</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éta próbka <b>vyvódit</b> menjá iz sebjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">This traffic jam <b>is driving</b> me <b>crazy</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выводить.html>выводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:терпение.html>терпе́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vyvodítʹ</b> iz terpénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make smb. lose patience, to exasperate smb.</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">to <b>remove</b> (someone) from patience</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выводить.html>выводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>стро́я</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vyvodítʹ</b> iz strója</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put out of action / operation / commission, to disable, to wreck</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">to <b>remove</b> from the order</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to extirpate, to destroy; to exterminate (pests); to remove (stains, pimples)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выводиться.html>выводи́ться</a> (27433)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выводить.html>выводи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vyvodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выводиться.html>выводи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vyvodítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вы́вестись</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become extinct</li>
<li>to go out of use, to fall into disuse</li>
<li>to come out, to go away <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of stains</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to hatch</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выводить.html>выводи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vyvodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***выводок.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выводок.html>вы́водок</a> (24418)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выводить.html>выводи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vyvodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ок</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with perfective-verb stress.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выводок.html>вы́водок</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vývodok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выводок.html>вы́водка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выводок.html>вы́водки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выводок.html>вы́водков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>brood, hatch, litter</li></ol>

***вывозить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вывозить.html>вы́возить</a> (8934)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возить.html>вози́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; by rule, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вы́-</span> attracts the stress in perfective but not imperfective verbs.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вывозить.html>вывози́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vyvozítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вывезти.html>вы́везти</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to take out (by vehicle), to remove
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вывозить.html>вывози́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тачка.html>та́чке</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">pejorative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vyvozítʹ na táčke</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to protest by removing someone in a wheelbarrow from an administrative post</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">to cart away in a wheelbarrow</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to deliver
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вывозить.html>вывози́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">dated<span class="ib-comma qualifier-comma">,</span> high-style</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vyvozítʹ v svet</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to introduce (young girls) to the community</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">to deliver into the light</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to export</li>
<li>to bring back</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rescue, to save</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">export</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:экспортировать.html>экспорти́ровать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">eksportírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">rescue</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выручать.html>выруча́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vyručátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выворачивать.html>вывора́чивать</a> (10622)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выворотить.html>вы́воротить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vývorotitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выворачивать.html>вывора́чивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vyvoráčivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выворотить.html>вы́воротить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to unscrew</li>
<li><i>(an arm, a leg etc.)</i> <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to twist, to wrench</li>
<li>to turn <i>(inside)</i> out</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">twist, turn inside out</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вывёртывать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vyvjórtyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***выгадать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выгадать.html>вы́гадать</a> (32190)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выгадать.html>вы́гадать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výgadatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">выга́дывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to gain
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́том</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выгадать.html>вы́гадал</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on na etom ne vygadal</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he gained nothing by / from it</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to economize, save</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выглядеть.html>вы́глядеть</a> (869)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глядеть.html>гляде́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gljadétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выглядеть.html>вы́глядеть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výgljadetʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to look, to appear, to seem
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стараться.html>стара́йся</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:выглядеть.html>вы́глядеть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:модный.html>мо́дно</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ne starájsja <b>výgljadetʹ</b> módno.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Don't try <b>to look</b> fashionable.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выглядеть.html>вы́глядеть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výgljadetʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выглядывать.html>выгля́дывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to find, to discover, to spy out</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выглядывать.html>выгля́дывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vygljádyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выглянуть.html>вы́глянуть</a></b>)

<li>to appear, to emerge, to come into view</li></ol>
